padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-398" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-399" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">+</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-400" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">6</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.215em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.302em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>×</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>×</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>;</mo><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>=</mo><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mo>+</mo><mn>6</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-33">\rm x+4\times\left(-1\right)+1\times\left(-2\right)=0;\therefore x-4-2=0\therefore x=\ +6 </script></span></p>

<p>[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪৬১]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: অর্থো-প্যারা নির্দেশক গ্রুপ-&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 14.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.191em, 1014.26em, 2.338em, -999.998em);                                     <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: Cr,Cu,Mo,Ag,La,Ac,Au ইত্যাদি ব্যতিক্রমধর্মী ইলেকট্রন বিন্যাস প্রদর্শন করে।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-২৬১]</p>
</span>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>ক্ষমতা = গতিশক্তির পরিবর্তন/সময় <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-97-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>249</mn><mn>6</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>41.5</mn><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>W</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-950" style="width: 6.928em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 5.658em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1005.66em, 2.502em, -999.998em); position: relative; width: 1.191em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.404em, 1001.03em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.531em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-954" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">249</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.33em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-955" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">6</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1001.19em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; [ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৩৭২]</p>

                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>until</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>as if</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>'since' এর পূর্বে Past Indefinite tense হলে since এর পরে Past Perfect tense হয়। until ও let alone এখানে সঙ্গতিপূর্ণ নয়। As if unreal past প্রকাশে ব্যবহৃত হয়।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>রোগে মারা গেলে die- এর সাথে of বসে। বেশি খেয়ে মারা গেলে die- এর সাথে from, ধীরে ধীরে বিলুপ্তি ঘটলে die- এর সাথে off এবং বিশেষ উদ্দেশ্যে নিজেকে আত্মনিয়োগ করে মারা গেলে die- এর সাথে for বসে।</p>

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 82 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Choose the correct indirect speech of the following sentences:&nbsp;<br>
He said to me, 'Are you ill?' I replied, 'No'.</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He asked me if I was ill. I replied that I was not.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He asked me if I was ill. I replied that I was.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He asked me that I am ill. I replied that I was.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He asked me that I am not ill. I replied I was not.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>প্রদত্ত বাক্যগুলোর প্রথমটি Interrogative হওয়ায় inverted comma- এর পরিবর্তে if হবে এবং দ্বিতীয় বাক্যটিতে Not থাকায় সেটি Negative structure- এ হবে। সে অনুযায়ী অপশন (a)-এর বাক্যটি উভয় শর্তই পূরণ করে, তাই এটি সঠিক উত্তর।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                            </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>to have been</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>to have had begun</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Voice- এর Passive- এর নিয়মে 'to have' থাকলে to have been + V এর Past Participle form বসে।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 87 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>The tree has been blown _____ by the strong wind.</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>away</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>up</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>off</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>out</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Blow away-অর্থ উপড়ে ফেলা বা এক স্থান থেকে অন্য স্থানে সরিয়ে নিয়ে যাওয়া (বাতাসের সাহায্যে)। Blow up অর্থ- বিস্ফোরক ব্যবহার করে ধ্বংস করা; Blow off অর্থ- ভেতর থেকে নির্গত হওয়া; Blow out অর্থ- আগুন নেভানো।&nbsp;</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Stout : weak</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>

                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Hook : Crook</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Harm অর্থ ক্ষতি করা আর Damage অর্থ ক্ষতি/অনিষ্ট করা পরস্পর সমার্থক শব্দ। একইভাবে Injure এবং Incapacitate উভয় শব্দের অর্থই শক্তি হরণ করা বা অনিষ্ট করা।</p>
</span>
